    38→function toPositiveInt(value, fallback) {
    39→  const n = Number(value);
    40→  return Number.isInteger(n) && n > 0 ? n : fallback;
    41→}
    42→
    43→function randomBetween(min, max) {
    44→  if (max <= min) return min;
    45→  return min + Math.floor(Math.random() * (max - min + 1));
    46→}
    47→
    48→function resolveDelayRange(sourceSite) {
    49→  const meta = sourceSite?.meta && typeof sourceSite.meta === "object" ? sourceSite.meta : {};
    50→  const baseDelay = toPositiveInt(meta.delay_ms, 1500);
    51→  const minDelay = toPositiveInt(meta.delay_min_ms, baseDelay);
    52→  const maxDelay = toPositiveInt(meta.delay_max_ms, Math.max(baseDelay, minDelay));
    53→  return {
    54→    min: Math.max(0, minDelay),
    55→    max: Math.max(minDelay, maxDelay),
    56→  };
    57→}

    60→  return sourceSiteStore.load(pg, sourceId);
    61→}

    63→async function fetchHtml(url, sourceSite) {
    64→  const options = buildSourceFetchOptions(sourceSite, config);
    65→  const response = await fetchTextResource(url, options);
    66→  return {
    67→    ok: response.ok,
    68→    status: response.status,
    69→    html: response.text.slice(0, 250000),
    70→    finalUrl: response.finalUrl || url,
    71→    fetchChannel: response.fetchChannel || "http",
    72→    decodedCharset: response.decodedCharset || "",
    73→    error: response.error,

    77→async function processClaimedTask(pg, redis, claimed) {
    78→  const taskId = requireString(claimed.id, "id");
    79→  const runId = String(claimed.run_id || "").trim();

    83→  const url = requireString(claimed.url, "url");
    84→

    86→    log(serviceName, "warn", "skip stale fetch task", {
    87→      taskId,

    93→  }
    94→
    95→  try {
    96→    const sourceSite = await loadSourceSite(pg, sourceId);
    97→    const nextAllowedAt = sourceNextAllowedAt.get(sourceId) ?? 0;
    98→    const waitMs = Math.max(0, nextAllowedAt - Date.now());
    99→    if (waitMs > 0) {

   101→    }

   111→      );
   112→    }
   113→

   117→         SET stage = $2,

   275→
   276→async function runLoop(pg, redis) {
   277→  let nextDatabaseSweepAt = 0;
   278→
   279→  while (!stopping) {
   280→    const now = Date.now();
   281→    const preferDatabase = now >= nextDatabaseSweepAt;
   282→    if (preferDatabase) {
   283→      nextDatabaseSweepAt = now + Math.max(1000, Number(config.fetchDbSweepIntervalMs ?? 5000));
   284→    }
   285→
   286→    const acquired = await withClaimGate(async () =>
   287→      acquireNextFetchTask(pg, redis, {
   288→        queueName: config.queues.fetch,
   289→        pollSeconds: config.pollSeconds,
   290→        leaseMs: config.fetchStaleAfterMs,
   291→        preferDatabase,
   292→        workerName: serviceName,
   293→        serviceName,
   294→        sourceInFlight,
   295→        popQueueImpl: popQueue,
   296→        pushQueueImpl: pushQueue,
   297→        sleepImpl: sleep,
   298→      })
   299→    );
   300→    if (!acquired) {
   301→      await sleep(150);
   302→      continue;
   303→    }
   304→
   305→    const sourceId = String(acquired.claimed?.source_id || "").trim();
   306→    try {
   307→      await processClaimedTask(pg, redis, acquired.claimed);
   308→    } catch (error) {
   309→      log(serviceName, "error", "process fetch message failed", {
   310→        error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
   311→        taskId: acquired.claimed?.id ?? null,
   312→        sourceId: acquired.claimed?.source_id ?? null,
   313→        origin: acquired.origin,
   314→      });
   315→    } finally {
   316→      if (sourceId) {
   317→        sourceInFlight.delete(sourceId);
   318→      }
   319→    }
   320→  }
   321→}
   322→
   323→async function withClaimGate(fn) {
   324→  const previous = claimGate;
   325→  let release;
   326→  claimGate = new Promise((resolve) => {
   327→    release = resolve;
   328→  });
   329→
   330→  await previous;
   331→  try {
   332→    return await fn();
   333→  } finally {
   334→    release();
   335→  }
   336→}

   338→async function runRecoveryLoop(pg, redis) {
   339→  const intervalMs = Math.max(1000, Number(config.fetchRecoveryIntervalMs ?? 30000));
   340→  while (!stopping) {
   341→    try {
   342→      const result = await recoverStaleFetchTasks(pg, redis, {
   343→        staleAfterMs: config.fetchStaleAfterMs,
   344→        batchSize: config.fetchRecoveryBatchSize,
   345→        queueName: config.queues.fetch,
   346→        workerName: serviceName,
   347→        pushQueueImpl: pushQueue,
   348→        recordPipelineEventImpl: recordPipelineEvent,
   349→      });
   350→      if (result.recoveredCount > 0) {
   351→        log(serviceName, "warn", "recovered stale fetching tasks", {
   352→          recoveredCount: result.recoveredCount,
   353→          taskIds: result.tasks.map((task) => task.id),
   354→        });
   355→      }
   356→    } catch (error) {
   357→      log(serviceName, "error", "recover stale fetching tasks failed", {
   358→        error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
   359→      });
   360→    }
   361→    await sleep(intervalMs);
   362→  }
   363→}
   364→
   365→async function main() {
   366→  const pg = createPgPool(config.db);
   367→  const redis = createRedisClient(config.redis);
   368→  try {
   369→    await ensurePlatformSchema(pg);
   370→    const loops = Array.from(
   371→      { length: Math.max(1, config.fetchConcurrency) },
   372→      () => runLoop(pg, redis)
   373→    );
   374→    loops.push(runRecoveryLoop(pg, redis));
   375→    await Promise.all(loops);
   376→  } finally {
   377→    await redis.quit();
   378→    await pg.end();
   379→  }
   380→}

   385→  });
   386→  process.exit(1);

    66→export function parseRobots(text, userAgent = "*") {
    67→  const groups = [];
    68→  let current = {
    69→    userAgents: [],
    70→    disallowRules: [],
    71→    allowRules: [],
    72→    crawlDelay: null,
    73→  };
    74→  const sitemaps = [];
    75→
    76→  const flushGroup = () => {
    77→    if (current.userAgents.length > 0) {
    78→      groups.push(current);
    79→    }
    80→    current = {
    81→      userAgents: [],
    82→      disallowRules: [],
    83→      allowRules: [],
    84→      crawlDelay: null,
    85→    };
    86→  };
    87→
    88→  const lines = String(text || "").split(/\r?\n/);
    89→  for (const rawLine of lines) {
    90→    const line = rawLine.replace(/#.*$/, "").trim();
    91→    if (!line) continue;
    92→    const index = line.indexOf(":");
    93→    if (index < 0) continue;
    94→    const key = line.slice(0, index).trim().toLowerCase();
    95→    const value = line.slice(index + 1).trim();
    96→
    97→    if (key === "sitemap") {
    98→      const loc = normalizeUrl(value);
    99→      if (loc) sitemaps.push(loc);
   100→      continue;
   101→    }
   102→
   103→    if (key === "user-agent") {
   104→      if (
   105→        current.userAgents.length > 0 &&
   106→        (current.disallowRules.length > 0 ||
   107→          current.allowRules.length > 0 ||
   108→          current.crawlDelay !== null)
   109→      ) {
   110→        flushGroup();
   111→      }
   112→      current.userAgents.push(value.toLowerCase());
   113→      continue;
   114→    }
   115→
   116→    if (key === "disallow") current.disallowRules.push(value);
   117→    if (key === "allow") current.allowRules.push(value);
   118→    if (key === "crawl-delay") {
   119→      const n = Number(value);
   120→      if (!Number.isNaN(n) && Number.isFinite(n)) current.crawlDelay = n;
   121→    }
   122→  }
   123→  flushGroup();
   124→
   125→  const targetUA = String(userAgent || "*").toLowerCase();
   126→  let selected = null;
   127→  let bestLen = 0;
   128→  for (const group of groups) {
   129→    for (const ua of group.userAgents) {
   130→      if (!ua) continue;
   131→      if (ua === "*") {
   132→        if (bestLen < 1) {
   133→          bestLen = 1;
   134→          selected = group;
   135→        }
   136→        continue;
   137→      }
   138→      if (targetUA.includes(ua) && ua.length > bestLen) {
   139→        bestLen = ua.length;
   140→        selected = group;
   141→      }
   142→    }
   143→  }
   144→
   145→  const disallowRules = selected?.disallowRules ?? [];
   146→  const allowRules = selected?.allowRules ?? [];
   147→  const crawlDelay = selected?.crawlDelay ?? null;
   148→  const disallowAll =
   149→    disallowRules.some((rule) => rule === "/") && !allowRules.some((rule) => rule === "/");
   150→
   151→  return {
   152→    sitemaps,
   153→    disallowRules,
   154→    allowRules,
   155→    crawlDelay,
   156→    disallowAll,
   157→  };
   158→}
   159→
   160→export function isRobotsAllowed(url, baseUrl, robotsMeta) {
   161→  if (!robotsMeta) return true;
   162→  if (robotsMeta.disallowAll) return false;
   163→
   164→  let target;
   165→  try {
   166→    target = new URL(url, baseUrl);
   167→  } catch {
   168→    return false;
   169→  }
   170→  const path = `${target.pathname}${target.search}`;
   171→  let allowLen = -1;
   172→  let disallowLen = -1;
   173→
   174→  for (const rule of robotsMeta.allowRules ?? []) {
   175→    if (rule && path.startsWith(rule) && rule.length > allowLen) {
   176→      allowLen = rule.length;
   177→    }
   178→  }
   179→  for (const rule of robotsMeta.disallowRules ?? []) {
   180→    if (rule && path.startsWith(rule) && rule.length > disallowLen) {
   181→      disallowLen = rule.length;
   182→    }
   183→  }
   184→
   185→  if (disallowLen < 0) return true;
   186→  if (allowLen >= disallowLen) return true;
   187→  return false;
   188→}

   190→export function parseSitemapLocs(xml) {
   191→  const locs = [];
   192→  const regex = /<loc>([\s\S]*?)<\/loc>/gi;
   193→  let match = regex.exec(xml);
   194→  while (match) {
   195→    const value = cleanText(htmlDecode(match[1]));
   196→    if (value) locs.push(value);
   197→    match = regex.exec(xml);
   198→  }
   199→  return locs;
   200→}
   201→
   202→export function extractAnchors(html, pageUrl) {
   203→  const anchors = [];
   204→  const seen = new Set();
   205→  const regex = /<a\b([^>]*)href=["']([^"']+)["']([^>]*)>([\s\S]*?)<\/a>/gi;
   206→  let match = regex.exec(html);
   207→  while (match) {
   208→    const href = normalizeUrl(htmlDecode(match[2]), pageUrl);
   209→    if (!href || seen.has(href)) {
   210→      match = regex.exec(html);
   211→      continue;
   212→    }
   213→    seen.add(href);
   214→    anchors.push({
   215→      href,
   216→      text: cleanText(match[4]),
   217→    });
   218→    match = regex.exec(html);
   219→  }
   220→  return anchors;
   221→}

   223→export function normalizeSourceSite(sourceSite, overrides = {}) {
   224→  const meta = sourceSite?.meta && typeof sourceSite.meta === "object" ? sourceSite.meta : {};
   225→  const baseUrl = normalizeUrl(sourceSite?.base_url ?? sourceSite?.baseUrl ?? meta.base_url ?? "");
   226→  const rawStartUrls =
   227→    sourceSite?.startUrls ??
   228→    sourceSite?.start_urls ??
   229→    meta.start_urls ??
   230→    meta.startUrls ??
   231→    (baseUrl ? [baseUrl] : []);
   232→  const rawDetailPatterns =
   233→    sourceSite?.detailPatterns ??
   234→    sourceSite?.detail_patterns ??
   235→    meta.detail_patterns ??
   236→    meta.include_patterns ??
   237→    [];
   238→  const rawDiscoveryPatterns =
   239→    sourceSite?.discoveryPatterns ?? sourceSite?.discovery_patterns ?? meta.discovery_patterns ?? [];
   240→  const rawExcludePatterns =
   241→    sourceSite?.excludePatterns ?? sourceSite?.exclude_patterns ?? meta.exclude_patterns ?? [];
   242→  const startUrls = [
   243→    ...new Set(
   244→      toArray(rawStartUrls)
   245→        .map((url) => normalizeUrl(url, baseUrl))
   246→        .filter(Boolean)
   247→    ),
   248→  ];
   249→
   250→  return {
   251→    id: String(sourceSite?.id || "").trim(),
   252→    name: String(sourceSite?.name || sourceSite?.id || "").trim(),
   253→    baseUrl,
   254→    startUrls,
   255→    detailPatterns: toArray(rawDetailPatterns),
   256→    discoveryPatterns: toArray(rawDiscoveryPatterns),
   257→    excludePatterns: toArray(rawExcludePatterns),
   258→    maxSitemaps: toPositiveInt(
   259→      overrides.maxSitemaps ?? sourceSite?.maxSitemaps ?? sourceSite?.max_sitemaps ?? meta.max_sitemaps,
   260→      2
   261→    ),
   262→    candidateLimit: toPositiveInt(
   263→      overrides.candidateLimitPerSource ??
   264→        sourceSite?.candidateLimit ??
   265→        sourceSite?.max_candidate_urls ??
   266→        meta.max_candidate_urls,
   267→      100
   268→    ),
   269→    discoveryPageLimit: toPositiveInt(
   270→      overrides.discoveryPageLimit ??
   271→        sourceSite?.discoveryPageLimit ??
   272→        sourceSite?.max_discovery_pages ??
   273→        meta.max_discovery_pages,
   274→      20
   275→    ),
   276→    renderViaPinchtab: Boolean(
   277→      sourceSite?.renderViaPinchtab ?? sourceSite?.render_via_pinchtab ?? meta.render_via_pinchtab ?? false
   278→    ),
   279→    pinchtabMode: String(
   280→      sourceSite?.pinchtabMode ??
   281→        sourceSite?.pinchtab_mode ??
   282→        meta.pinchtab_mode ??
   283→        "fallback"
   284→    ),
   285→    crawlDelayMs: toPositiveInt(sourceSite?.crawlDelayMs ?? sourceSite?.delay_ms ?? meta.delay_ms, 1500),
   286→    crawlDelayMinMs: toPositiveInt(
   287→      sourceSite?.crawlDelayMinMs ?? sourceSite?.delay_min_ms ?? meta.delay_min_ms,
   288→      0
   289→    ),
   290→    crawlDelayMaxMs: toPositiveInt(
   291→      sourceSite?.crawlDelayMaxMs ?? sourceSite?.delay_max_ms ?? meta.delay_max_ms,
   292→      0
   293→    ),
   294→  };
   295→}

   297→export function isDetailCandidate(url, sourceSite, robotsMeta) {
   298→  if (!url || !sourceSite.baseUrl) return false;
   299→  if (!isSameOrigin(url, sourceSite.baseUrl)) return false;
   300→  if (!isRobotsAllowed(url, sourceSite.baseUrl, robotsMeta)) return false;
   301→  if (matchesAny(url, sourceSite.excludePatterns)) return false;
   302→  if (sourceSite.detailPatterns.length === 0) return false;
   303→  return matchesAny(url, sourceSite.detailPatterns);
   304→}
   305→
   306→export function isDiscoveryCandidate(url, sourceSite, robotsMeta) {
   307→  if (!url || !sourceSite.baseUrl) return false;
   308→  if (!isSameOrigin(url, sourceSite.baseUrl)) return false;
   309→  if (!isRobotsAllowed(url, sourceSite.baseUrl, robotsMeta)) return false;
   310→  if (matchesAny(url, sourceSite.excludePatterns)) return false;
   311→  if (isDetailCandidate(url, sourceSite, robotsMeta)) return false;
   312→  if (sourceSite.discoveryPatterns.length === 0) {
   313→    return sourceSite.startUrls.some((seed) => url.startsWith(seed));
   314→  }
   315→  return matchesAny(url, sourceSite.discoveryPatterns);
   316→}

   318→export async function discoverSourceCandidates(options) {
   319→  const sourceSite = normalizeSourceSite(options.sourceSite, options.overrides);
   320→  const fetchPlainText = options.fetchPlainText;
   321→  const fetchHtmlPage = options.fetchHtmlPage;
   322→  const userAgent = String(options.userAgent || "*");
   323→  const onCandidates = typeof options.onCandidates === "function" ? options.onCandidates : null;
   324→  const shouldContinue = typeof options.shouldContinue === "function" ? options.shouldContinue : null;
   325→  const candidateBatchSize = toPositiveInt(options.candidateBatchSize, 100);
   326→  const summary = {
   327→    sourceId: sourceSite.id,
   328→    robotsUrl: sourceSite.baseUrl ? new URL("/robots.txt", sourceSite.baseUrl).toString() : "",
   329→    robotsFetched: false,
   330→    robotsDisallowAll: false,
   331→    sitemapFetchedCount: 0,
   332→    discoveryPageFetchedCount: 0,
   333→    candidateCount: 0,
   334→    candidateUrls: [],
   335→    errors: [],
   336→    stoppedReason: null,
   337→  };
   338→  const pendingCandidates = [];
   339→
   340→  async function continueDiscovery() {
   341→    if (!shouldContinue) return true;
   342→    return (await shouldContinue()) !== false;
   343→  }
   344→
   345→  async function flushCandidates(force = false) {
   346→    if (!onCandidates || pendingCandidates.length === 0) return;
   347→    if (!force && pendingCandidates.length < candidateBatchSize) return;
   348→    const batch = pendingCandidates.splice(0, pendingCandidates.length);
   349→    await onCandidates(batch);
   350→  }
   351→
   352→  async function addCandidate(url) {
   353→    if (!url || candidates.has(url)) return false;
   354→    candidates.add(url);
   355→    pendingCandidates.push(url);
   356→    await flushCandidates(false);
   357→    return true;
   358→  }
   359→
   360→  let robotsMeta = null;
   361→  if (summary.robotsUrl) {
   362→    const robotsRes = await fetchPlainText(summary.robotsUrl);
   363→    summary.robotsFetched = robotsRes.ok;
   364→    if (robotsRes.ok) {
   365→      robotsMeta = parseRobots(robotsRes.text, userAgent);
   366→      summary.robotsDisallowAll = robotsMeta.disallowAll;
   367→    } else if (robotsRes.error) {
   368→      summary.errors.push(`robots: ${robotsRes.error}`);
   369→    }
   370→  }
   371→
   372→  if (robotsMeta?.disallowAll) {
   373→    return summary;
   374→  }
   375→
   376→  const candidates = new Set();
   377→  const sitemapQueue = [...(robotsMeta?.sitemaps ?? [])];
   378→  const seenSitemaps = new Set();
   379→  const discoveryQueue = [...sourceSite.startUrls];
   380→  const seenDiscoveryPages = new Set();
   381→
   382→  while (
   383→    sitemapQueue.length > 0 &&
   384→    seenSitemaps.size < sourceSite.maxSitemaps &&
   385→    candidates.size < sourceSite.candidateLimit
   386→  ) {
   387→    if (!(await continueDiscovery())) {
   388→      summary.stoppedReason = "inactive_run";
   389→      break;
   390→    }
   391→    const sitemapUrl = sitemapQueue.shift();
   392→    if (!sitemapUrl || seenSitemaps.has(sitemapUrl)) continue;
   393→    seenSitemaps.add(sitemapUrl);
   394→
   395→    const sitemapRes = await fetchPlainText(sitemapUrl);
   396→    if (!sitemapRes.ok) {
   397→      if (sitemapRes.error) {
   398→        summary.errors.push(`sitemap ${sitemapUrl}: ${sitemapRes.error}`);
   399→      }
   400→      continue;
   401→    }
   402→    summary.sitemapFetchedCount += 1;
   403→
   404→    for (const loc of parseSitemapLocs(sitemapRes.text)) {
   405→      if (looksLikeSitemap(loc)) {
   406→        if (!seenSitemaps.has(loc) && sitemapQueue.length + seenSitemaps.size < sourceSite.maxSitemaps * 4) {
   407→          sitemapQueue.push(loc);
   408→        }
   409→        continue;
   410→      }
   411→      if (isDetailCandidate(loc, sourceSite, robotsMeta)) {
   412→        await addCandidate(loc);
   413→        if (candidates.size >= sourceSite.candidateLimit) break;
   414→        continue;
   415→      }
   416→      if (isDiscoveryCandidate(loc, sourceSite, robotsMeta)) {
   417→        discoveryQueue.push(loc);
   418→      }
   419→    }
   420→  }
   421→
   422→  while (
   423→    discoveryQueue.length > 0 &&
   424→    seenDiscoveryPages.size < sourceSite.discoveryPageLimit &&
   425→    candidates.size < sourceSite.candidateLimit
   426→  ) {
   427→    if (!(await continueDiscovery())) {
   428→      summary.stoppedReason = "inactive_run";
   429→      break;
   430→    }
   431→    const pageUrl = discoveryQueue.shift();
   432→    if (!pageUrl || seenDiscoveryPages.has(pageUrl)) continue;
   433→    seenDiscoveryPages.add(pageUrl);
   434→
   435→    const pageRes = await fetchHtmlPage(pageUrl);
   436→    if (!pageRes.ok || !String(pageRes.contentType || "").toLowerCase().includes("html")) {
   437→      if (pageRes.error) {
   438→        summary.errors.push(`discover ${pageUrl}: ${pageRes.error}`);
   439→      }
   440→      continue;
   441→    }
   442→    summary.discoveryPageFetchedCount += 1;
   443→
   444→    for (const anchor of extractAnchors(pageRes.text, pageUrl)) {
   445→      if (isDetailCandidate(anchor.href, sourceSite, robotsMeta)) {
   446→        await addCandidate(anchor.href);
   447→        if (candidates.size >= sourceSite.candidateLimit) break;
   448→        continue;
   449→      }
   450→      if (
   451→        isDiscoveryCandidate(anchor.href, sourceSite, robotsMeta) &&
   452→        !seenDiscoveryPages.has(anchor.href) &&
   453→        discoveryQueue.length + seenDiscoveryPages.size < sourceSite.discoveryPageLimit * 4
   454→      ) {
   455→        discoveryQueue.push(anchor.href);
   456→      }
   457→    }
   458→  }
   459→
   460→  await flushCandidates(true);
   461→  summary.candidateUrls = [...candidates].slice(0, sourceSite.candidateLimit);
   462→  summary.candidateCount = summary.candidateUrls.length;
   463→  return summary;
   464→}

    14→export async function releaseFetchTaskClaim(pg, task, options = {}) {

    16→  const traceId = String(task?.trace_id || "").trim();

    41→    return;
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  if (!queueName) {
    45→    throw new Error("queueName is required when requeue is enabled");
    46→  }
    47→  if (typeof pushQueueImpl !== "function") {
    48→    throw new Error("pushQueueImpl is required when requeue is enabled");
    49→  }
    50→
    51→  await pushQueueImpl(options.redis, queueName, {
    52→    traceId,
    53→    jobId,
    54→    taskId,
    55→    sourceId,
    56→    url,
    57→    ...(runId ? { runId } : {}),
    58→  });
    59→}
    60→
    61→async function releaseIfSourceBusy(pg, redis, task, options = {}) {
    62→  const sourceId = String(task?.source_id || "").trim();
    63→  const sourceInFlight = options.sourceInFlight instanceof Set ? options.sourceInFlight : new Set();
    64→  const sleepImpl = options.sleepImpl;
    65→
    66→  if (!sourceId || !sourceInFlight.has(sourceId)) {
    67→    return false;
    68→  }
    69→
    70→  await releaseFetchTaskClaim(pg, task, {
    71→    reason: "requeued because source is already in flight",
    72→    requeue: Boolean(options.requeue),
    73→    queueName: options.queueName,
    74→    pushQueueImpl: options.pushQueueImpl,
    75→    redis,
    76→  });
    77→  if (typeof sleepImpl !== "function") {
    78→    throw new Error("sleepImpl is required when releasing a busy source");
    79→  }
    80→  await sleepImpl(CLAIM_RETRY_DELAY_MS);
    81→  return true;
    82→}
    83→
    84→async function claimFromDatabase(pg, redis, options = {}) {
    85→  const claimed = await options.claimNextQueuedFetchTaskImpl(pg, {
    86→    leaseMs: options.leaseMs,
    87→    workerName: options.workerName,
    88→    excludeSourceIds: [...options.sourceInFlight],
    89→  });
    90→  if (!claimed) {
    91→    return null;
    92→  }
    93→
    94→  const released = await releaseIfSourceBusy(pg, redis, claimed, {
    95→    sourceInFlight: options.sourceInFlight,
    96→    requeue: false,
    97→    queueName: options.queueName,
    98→    pushQueueImpl: options.pushQueueImpl,
    99→    sleepImpl: options.sleepImpl,
   100→  });
   101→  if (released) {
   102→    return null;
   103→  }
   104→
   105→  const sourceId = String(claimed?.source_id || "").trim();
   106→  if (sourceId) {
   107→    options.sourceInFlight.add(sourceId);
   108→  }
   109→
   110→  return {
   111→    claimed,
   112→    origin: "database",
   113→    message: null,
   114→  };
   115→}
   116→
   117→export async function acquireNextFetchTask(pg, redis, options = {}) {
   118→  const queueName = requireNonEmptyString(options.queueName, "queueName");
   119→  const pollSeconds = Number(options.pollSeconds) > 0 ? Number(options.pollSeconds) : 5;
   120→  const leaseMs = Number(options.leaseMs) > 0 ? Number(options.leaseMs) : 60000;
   121→  const workerName = String(options.workerName || "worker-fetch-http").trim();
   122→  const serviceName = String(options.serviceName || workerName).trim();
   123→  const sourceInFlight = options.sourceInFlight instanceof Set ? options.sourceInFlight : new Set();
   124→  const popQueueImpl = options.popQueueImpl;
   125→  const pushQueueImpl = options.pushQueueImpl;
   126→  const sleepImpl = options.sleepImpl;
   127→  const claimFetchTaskImpl = options.claimFetchTaskImpl ?? claimFetchTask;
   128→  const claimNextQueuedFetchTaskImpl = options.claimNextQueuedFetchTaskImpl ?? claimNextQueuedFetchTask;
   129→
   130→  if (typeof popQueueImpl !== "function") {
   131→    throw new Error("popQueueImpl is required");
   132→  }
   133→  if (typeof pushQueueImpl !== "function") {
   134→    throw new Error("pushQueueImpl is required");
   135→  }
   136→  if (typeof sleepImpl !== "function") {
   137→    throw new Error("sleepImpl is required");
   138→  }
   139→
   140→  if (options.preferDatabase) {
   141→    const claimedFromDatabase = await claimFromDatabase(pg, redis, {
   142→      queueName,
   143→      leaseMs,
   144→      workerName,
   145→      sourceInFlight,
   146→      pushQueueImpl,
   147→      sleepImpl,
   148→      claimNextQueuedFetchTaskImpl,
   149→    });
   150→    if (claimedFromDatabase) {
   151→      return claimedFromDatabase;
   152→    }
   153→  }
   154→
   155→  const message = await popQueueImpl(redis, queueName, pollSeconds);
   156→  if (message) {
   157→    const messageSourceId = String(message?.sourceId || "").trim();
   158→    if (messageSourceId && sourceInFlight.has(messageSourceId)) {
   159→      await pushQueueImpl(redis, queueName, message);
   160→      await sleepImpl(CLAIM_RETRY_DELAY_MS);
   161→      return null;
   162→    }
   163→
   164→    const taskId = requireNonEmptyString(message?.taskId, "taskId");
   165→    const claimed = await claimFetchTaskImpl(pg, taskId, {
   166→      leaseMs,
   167→      workerName,
   168→    });
   169→    if (!claimed) {
   170→      return null;
   171→    }
   172→
   173→    const released = await releaseIfSourceBusy(pg, redis, claimed, {
   174→      sourceInFlight,
   175→      requeue: true,
   176→      queueName,
   177→      pushQueueImpl,
   178→      sleepImpl,
   179→    });
   180→    if (released) {
   181→      return null;
   182→    }
   183→
   184→    const claimedSourceId = String(claimed?.source_id || messageSourceId).trim();
   185→    if (claimedSourceId) {
   186→      sourceInFlight.add(claimedSourceId);
   187→    }
   188→
   189→    return {
   190→      claimed,
   191→      origin: "queue",
   192→      message,
   193→    };
   194→  }
   195→
   196→  return claimFromDatabase(pg, redis, {
   197→    queueName,
   198→    leaseMs,
   199→    workerName,
   200→    sourceInFlight,
   201→    pushQueueImpl,
   202→    sleepImpl,
   203→    claimNextQueuedFetchTaskImpl,
   204→  });
   205→}

    76→async function processMessage(pg, redis, message) {

   176→async function runLoop(pg, redis) {
   177→  while (!stopping) {
   178→    const message = await popQueue(redis, config.queues.discovery, config.pollSeconds);
   179→    if (!message) {
   180→      await sleep(150);
   181→      continue;
   182→    }
   183→    try {
   184→      await processMessage(pg, redis, message);
   185→    } catch (error) {
   186→      log(serviceName, "error", "process discovery message failed", {
   187→        error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
   188→        message,
   189→      });
   190→    }
   191→  }
   192→}
   193→
   194→async function main() {
   195→  const pg = createPgPool(config.db);
   196→  const redis = createRedisClient(config.redis);
   197→  try {
   198→    await ensurePlatformSchema(pg);
   199→    const loops = Array.from(
   200→      { length: Math.max(1, config.discoveryConcurrency) },
   201→      () => runLoop(pg, redis)
   202→    );
   203→    await Promise.all(loops);
   204→  } finally {
   205→    await redis.quit();
   206→    await pg.end();
   207→  }
   208→}

   212→    error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error),
   213→  });
   214→  process.exit(1);

    84→export async function recoverStaleFetchTasks(pg, redis, options = {}) {
    85→  const staleAfterMs = toPositiveInt(options.staleAfterMs, 0);
    86→  const batchSize = toPositiveInt(options.batchSize, 20);
    87→  const queueName = String(options.queueName || "").trim();
    88→  const workerName = String(options.workerName || "worker-fetch-http").trim();

    90→  const recordPipelineEventImpl = options.recordPipelineEventImpl;

    92→  if (
    93→    staleAfterMs <= 0 ||
    94→    batchSize <= 0 ||
    95→    !queueName ||
    96→    typeof pushQueueImpl !== "function" ||
    97→    typeof recordPipelineEventImpl !== "function"
    98→  ) {

   101→

   103→    `WITH stale AS (
   104→       SELECT id, run_id, trace_id, job_id, source_id, url
   105→       FROM crawl_tasks
   106→       WHERE status = $1
   107→         AND COALESCE(fetch_lease_expires_at, updated_at + ($2::bigint * INTERVAL '1 millisecond')) < NOW()
   108→       ORDER BY COALESCE(fetch_lease_expires_at, updated_at) ASC
   109→       LIMIT $3
   110→       FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED
   111→     )
   112→     UPDATE crawl_tasks AS t
   113→     SET stage = $4,
   114→         status = $5,

   117→         fetch_worker = NULL,

   120→         updated_at = NOW()
   121→     FROM stale
   122→     WHERE t.id = stale.id
   123→     RETURNING stale.id, stale.run_id, stale.trace_id, stale.job_id, stale.source_id, stale.url`,
   124→    [
   125→      STATUS_FETCHING,
   126→      staleAfterMs,
   127→      batchSize,
   128→      FETCH_STAGE,
   129→      STATUS_QUEUED_FETCH,
   130→      "requeued after stale fetch timeout",
   131→    ]
   132→  );
   133→
   134→  const tasks = res.rows ?? [];
   135→  for (const task of tasks) {
   136→    await pushQueueImpl(redis, queueName, {
   137→      traceId: task.trace_id,
   138→      jobId: task.job_id,
   139→      taskId: task.id,
   140→      sourceId: task.source_id,
   141→      url: task.url,
   142→      ...(task.run_id ? { runId: task.run_id } : {}),
   143→    });
   144→    await recordPipelineEventImpl(pg, {
   145→      runId: task.run_id ?? null,
   146→      traceId: task.trace_id,
   147→      jobId: task.job_id,
   148→      taskId: task.id,
   149→      worker: workerName,
   150→      name: "fetch_requeued_stale",
   151→      payload: {
   152→        sourceId: task.source_id,
   153→        url: task.url,
   154→        queue: queueName,
   155→        staleAfterMs,
   156→      },
   157→    });
   158→  }
   159→
   160→  return {
   161→    recoveredCount: tasks.length,
   162→    tasks,
   163→  };
   164→}

assistant #32 10:20:20

Found it. Here's the situation:

11.md 第 28-29 行说得很清楚：claimNextQueuedFetchTask 的 SQL 没有 LIMIT 1，DB sweep 一次会把整批 queued_fetch 全部改成 fetching。

看 fetch-recovery.mjs:68-82，claimNextQueuedFetchTask 构造的 selector SQL 是：

SELECT id, run_id, trace_id, job_id, source_id, url
FROM crawl_tasks
WHERE status = $1
  AND source_id <> ALL($2::text[])
ORDER BY last_fetch_enqueue_at ASC NULLS FIRST, created_at ASC

然后传给 claimQueuedFetchTask，它在外面包了 FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED 和一个 CTE UPDATE ... FROM target WHERE t.id = target.id。

问题：没有 LIMIT 1，这个 CTE 会选中所有 queued_fetch 状态的行，然后一次性全部 UPDATE 成 fetching。虽然 RETURNING 只返回行，claimQueuedFetchTask 只取 res.rows[0]，但 UPDATE 已经把整批都改了。剩下的任务全部卡在 fetching 状态，没有 worker 在处理它们。

修复很简单：给 selector SQL 加 LIMIT 1。

Tool Call #33 Edit tooluse_3nnoDcUF64SisPcxDffrbG 10:20:20
Edit input={"file_path":"d:\\demo1\\papaweb\\services\\worker-fetch-http\\src\\fetch-recovery.mjs","new_string":" FROM crawl_tasks\n WHERE status = $1\n AND source_id <> ALL($2::text[])\n ...
Show input payload 
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "d:\\demo1\\papaweb\\services\\worker-fetch-http\\src\\fetch-recovery.mjs",
  "old_string": "     FROM crawl_tasks\n     WHERE status = $1\n       AND source_id <> ALL($2::text[])\n     ORDER BY last_fetch_enqueue_at ASC NULLS FIRST, created_at ASC`,",
  "new_string": "     FROM crawl_tasks\n     WHERE status = $1\n       AND source_id <> ALL($2::text[])\n     ORDER BY last_fetch_enqueue_at ASC NULLS FIRST, created_at ASC\n     LIMIT 1`,"
}

assistant #47 10:22:17

全部测试通过。来总结一下当前进度：

根据 11.md 的记录，你们的冷启动压测一路打出了三个关键缺陷，逐个修复：

1. 旧 run 外键穿透 — discovery 侧补了 isDiscoveryJobActive 保护，onCandidates 和 shouldContinue 都会检查 job 是否仍存在。已提交在 c297839。

2. fetch claim 并发竞态 — 多个循环同时 claim 同一 source 的任务。修复方案是 withClaimGate 串行化 + sourceInFlight Set 在 acquire 内部就标记。代码已写好，未提交。

3. claimNextQueuedFetchTask 缺少 LIMIT 1 — 这是刚才修的最后一个根因。DB sweep 的 CTE 没有 LIMIT 1，一次把所有 queued_fetch 行都 UPDATE 成 fetching，但只返回第一行给 worker 处理，剩下的全部成了孤儿。现在已加上 LIMIT 1。

当前状态：三个缺陷的代码修复都已就绪，测试全绿（discovery 6 pass，fetch-http 11 pass）。未提交的变更涵盖 7 个文件。

下一步就是重建 worker-fetch-http 镜像、部署、再起一轮三平台 run 验证 fetch claim 不再批量打穿。要我帮你提交这批变更吗？

Any in-flight queue messages from a prior run that don't match the new `runId` will be rejected by workers via `isSourceRunActive()`.\n\n2. `resetPipelineSources(pg, redis, { sourceIds, queues })` — runs a Postgres transaction that hard-deletes all prior data for the given `sourceIds`:\n   - `pipeline_events`\n   - `quality_scores`\n   - `gold_tool_entities`\n   - `url_state`\n   - `seed_state`\n   - `crawl_tasks`\n   - `crawl_jobs` (orphaned ones only)\n\n   Then for every Redis queue in `config.queues`, it calls `pruneQueueMessagesBySourceIds()` which does `LRANGE` + `DEL` + `RPUSH` (atomic via `MULTI/EXEC`) to strip all messages belonging to those `sourceIds`.\n\n3. Then enqueues a fresh discovery or seed batch with the new `runId` and `coldStart: true` propagated into every job/task/queue payload.\n\n---\n\n**The three callers**\n\n1. Airflow DAG — `d:/demo1/papaweb/services/orchestrator-airflow/dags/papaweb_platform_seed_pipeline.py`\n   Runs on a `*/30 * * * *` schedule. Does NOT pass `coldStart`, so it's a warm incremental run:\n   ```python\n   _http_post(\"/api/v1/pipeline/seed-run\", {\n     \"requestedBy\": \"airflow\",\n     \"reason\": \"scheduled_seed_pipeline\",\n   })\n   ```\n\n2. PowerShell smoke script — `d:/demo1/papaweb/infra/docker/platform-smoke.ps1`\n   Also no `coldStart`, used for post-deploy verification:\n   ```powershell\n   Invoke-RestMethod -Uri $triggerUrl -Method Post -Body (@{\n     requestedBy = \"platform-smoke\"\n     reason      = \"smoke_check\"\n   } | ConvertTo-Json)\n   ```\n\n3. Direct HTTP call (manual or test) — to trigger a cold start for multiple platforms:\n   ```bash\n   curl -X POST http://127.0.0.1:18787/api/v1/pipeline/seed-run \\\n     -H \"Content-Type: application/json\" \\\n     -d '{\n       \"coldStart\": true,\n       \"sourceIds\": [\"futurepedia\", \"toolify\", \"ainav_cn\"],\n       \"runId\": \"run_cold_001\",\n       \"requestedBy\": \"manual\",\n       \"reason\": \"cold_start_stress\"\n     }'\n   ```\n\n   The `sourceIds` array is what drives multi-platform scope. `collectRunSourceIds()` in `d:/demo1/papaweb/packages/shared/src/run-isolation.mjs` dedupes and normalizes them from either the request body or the seed plan's `sourceSites`/`targets`.\n\n---\n\n**Key files**\n\n- `d:/demo1/papaweb/services/query-api/src/index.mjs` — the endpoint handler (lines 116-196)\n- `d:/demo1/papaweb/packages/shared/src/run-isolation.mjs` — `preparePipelineRun`, `resetPipelineSources`, `pruneQueueMessagesBySourceIds`, `collectRunSourceIds`\n- `d:/demo1/papaweb/services/orchestrator-airflow/dags/papaweb_platform_seed_pipeline.py` — scheduled warm trigger\n- `d:/demo1/papaweb/infra/docker/platform-smoke.ps1` — smoke-check warm trigger\n\nThe `coldStart` flag is the exact boolean that gates the reset+isolation path. Without it, the endpoint just enqueues a new seed batch on top of existing state.",

+async function isDiscoveryJobActive(pg, jobId, runId) {
+  const normalizedRunId = String(runId || "").trim() || null;
+  const res = await pg.query(
+    `SELECT 1
+     FROM crawl_jobs
+     WHERE id = $1
+       AND run_id IS NOT DISTINCT FROM $2
+     LIMIT 1`,
+    [jobId, normalizedRunId]
+  );
+  return res.rowCount > 0;
+}

+async function withClaimGate(fn) {
+  const previous = claimGate;
+  let release;
+  claimGate = new Promise((resolve) => {
+    release = resolve;
+  });
+
+  await previous;
+  try {
+    return await fn();
+  } finally {
+    release();
+  }

assistant #120 11:22:57

提交完成。现在用大白话解释一下那些指标和修复：

---

想象你开了三家外卖店（futurepedia、toolify、ainav_cn），每家店都有一堆订单要处理。

指标解读：

fetching ≤1/source — 以前的 bug 是：厨房一次把所有订单都标成"正在做"，但实际只有一个厨师在干活，剩下几百单全卡住没人管。现在修好了，每家店同一时刻最多只有 1 单在做，做完一单再接下一单。

published 在增长，queued_fetch 在减少 — published 就是"已送达"的订单，queued_fetch 是"排队等做"的订单。数字说明三家店都在稳定出餐，队伍在缩短，流水线是通的。

三个 bug 通俗版：

1. 旧订单炸外键 — 你重新开店（冷启动），把旧菜单全删了。但之前的服务员还在往厨房送旧菜单上的菜，厨房一看"这菜单不存在啊"就报错崩了。修法：服务员送菜之前先看一眼菜单还在不在，不在就别送了。

2. 抢单竞态 — 好几个厨师同时看到同一家店的订单，一窝蜂全去抢。结果同一家店的菜被好几个人同时做，乱套了。修法：排队领单，一个一个来，领到了才标记"我在做这家的"。

3. LIMIT 1 缺失 — 这是最狠的 bug。厨师说"给我一单"，结果系统把整个队列几百单全标成"正在做"，但只把第一单交给厨师。剩下几百单全变成了没人管的孤儿。修法：SQL 加一句 LIMIT 1，一次只拿一单。

  "content": "# Cold-Start Stress Testing Fixes (2026-03-15)\n\nBranch: `feature/platform-cold-start-stress`\nPR: #6 merged to dev\n\n## Background\n三平台 (futurepedia, toolify, ainav_cn) 冷启动压测，逐步打出并修复了三个并发/竞态缺陷。\n\n## Bug 1: 旧 run 外键穿透\n- **现象**: 冷启动删除旧 job 后，旧 run 的 discovery 消息晚到，往 crawl_tasks 写入时 job_id 外键失败\n- **根因**: discovery 只检查 `isSourceRunActive`，没检查 job 是否还存在\n- **修复**:\n  - 新增 `isDiscoveryJobActive(pg, jobId, runId)` 函数\n  - `discoverSourceCandidates` 增加 `shouldContinue` 回调，每批 sitemap/page 前检查\n  - `onCandidates` 回调实现流式入队，入队前双重检查 run + job 存活\n- **文件**: `worker-discovery/src/index.mjs`, `packages/shared/src/discovery.mjs`\n\n## Bug 2: fetch claim 并发竞态\n- **现象**: 同一 source 的大量任务被多个 runLoop 同时 claim\n- **根因**: `sourceInFlight.add()` 在 `acquireNextFetchTask` 返回后才执行，多个循环在窗口期内同时通过 in-flight 检查\n- **修复**:\n  - `sourceInFlight.add()` 移入 `acquireNextFetchTask` 内部（claim 成功后立即标记）\n  - 新增 `withClaimGate` 串行化，用 Promise 链保证同一时刻只有一个 claim 操作\n- **文件**: `worker-fetch-http/src/fetch-claim.mjs`, `worker-fetch-http/src/index.mjs`\n\n## Bug 3: claimNextQueuedFetchTask 缺少 LIMIT 1\n- **现象**: 成百上千条任务瞬间变成 fetching，但只有一条被实际处理\n- **根因**: `claimNextQueuedFetchTask` 的 SELECT CTE 没有 `LIMIT 1`，`FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED` + `UPDATE FROM target` 会把所有匹配行都更新\n- **修复**: 在 ORDER BY 后加 `LIMIT 1`\n- **文件**: `worker-fetch-http/src/fetch-recovery.mjs:78-79`\n\n## 附带修复\n- `publish_worker`: job 更新加 `AND j.status <> 'discovering'`，防止 discovery 还在跑时被提前标记 completed\n- `ci.yml`: 加 `npm install` 步骤，修复 CI 找不到 pg 模块的问题\n\n## 验证方法\n触发冷启动后查询:\n```sql\nSELECT source_id, status, COUNT(*) FROM crawl_tasks\nWHERE run_id = '<run_id>'\nGROUP BY source_id, status ORDER BY source_id, status;\n```\n正常表现: 每个 source 的 `fetching` 始终 ≤1，`published` 稳步增长，`queued_fetch` 逐步减少。\n"

   144→## 技术架构要点
   145→
   146→### 四层架构
   147→
   148→```
   149→[自研 Web 前端]
   150→    ↓
   151→[适配网关层]（核心中枢）
   152→    ├── 轻量模式 → [大模型 API 直连]
   153→    └── 高级模式 → [OpenClaw] → [CLI Gateway] → [Workflow Engine]
   154→    ↓
   155→[Gitea（唯一数据底座）] + [索引层]
   156→```
   157→
   158→### 架构红线规则（11 条）
   159→
   160→Plan9 的 8 条 + Plan10 新增 3 条：
   161→1. 关键状态写必须经适配网关层或 CLI Gateway
   162→2. 工作流层仅调用已发布且版本冻结的插件
   163→3. 所有写操作必须可追溯
   164→4. audit replay 默认 dry-run
   165→5. 采集一期必须具备：账号池、代理池、会话租约、断点续爬
   166→6. 免费试用默认只读
   167→7. 合规边界优先
   168→8. 密钥零硬编码
   169→9. **（新增）前端不直接暴露 Gateway 地址**
   170→10. **（新增）会话存储格式不可随意变更**
   171→11. **（新增）禁止修改 OpenClaw 底层代码**

这个 Plan11 是 AgentCrawl 产品的宏观路线图（18 个月），而我们实际在做的是 papaweb 平台的数据采集流水线（对应 Phase 2 Week 17-20 的"官方数据采集插件"部分）。

从我们刚完成的工作来看，当前进度是：

已完成：
- 数据采集核心流水线：discovery → fetch → normalize → quality → publish 全链路
- 冷启动 run 隔离机制
- 三个并发/竞态 bug 修复（PR #6 已合并到 dev）
- CI/CD 基础（ci.yml + e2e.yml）
- 三平台压测验证通过（futurepedia, toolify, ainav_cn）

接下来可以做的方向：

1. 稳定性加固 — 继续跑更长时间的压测，观察全量消化完队列后 job 状态是否正确收尾（completed）
2. 产量/质量分析 — 分析已 published 的数据质量，看 normalize 和 quality 环节的表现
3. 更多平台接入 — 在 source-sites.v1.json 里加更多数据源
4. 监控告警 — Prometheus/Grafana 面板配置，对接 alertmanager
5. e2e 测试补全 — 让 e2e workflow 真正跑起来

你想先做哪个方向？

     9→- Monorepo with npm workspaces
    10→- All platform workers share same Docker image: `platform-runtime.Dockerfile`
    11→- Compose files in `infra/docker/`: `compose.base.yml`, `compose.platform.yml`, `compose.collect.yml`, `compose.observability.yml`, `compose.orchestrator.yml`
    12→- Build/restart single worker: `docker compose -f compose.base.yml -f compose.platform.yml build <service> && docker compose -f compose.base.yml -f compose.platform.yml up -d <service>`
    13→- 验证容器代码: `docker exec <container> grep <pattern> <file>`
    14→
    15→## Key Services
    16→- `query-api` (port 18787): API 入口，含 seed-run 触发端点
    17→- `worker-discovery`: 发现候选 URL
    18→- `worker-fetch-http`: 抓取页面

assistant #326 13:15:55

现在看清楚了。loadSeedPlan 有三种模式：

1. source_sites_config — 从 source-sites.v1.json 读取配置，走 discovery（sitemap + HTML 页面发现候选 URL）。这是我们一直在测的。
2. explicit_urls — 直接传入 seedUrls 列表，跳过 discovery，直接进 fetch 队列。
3. fallback — 前两种都没数据时的兜底。

让我再看看 query-api 的 seed-run 端点怎么路由这三种模式。

assistant #329 13:16:15

现在清楚了。seed-run 端点有两条路径：

1. source_sites_config 模式 — 有 sourceSites 时走 enqueueDiscoveryBatch，先 discovery 再 fetch。这是我们一直在测的。
2. explicit_urls 模式 — 传 seedUrls 时走 enqueueSeedBatch，跳过 discovery 直接进 fetch 队列。
3. fallback 模式 — 兜底，也走 enqueueSeedBatch。

我们只测了第一种（discovery 模式）。还需要测：

- explicit_urls — 直接传 URL 列表，验证跳过 discovery 直接 fetch → normalize → quality → publish 的链路
- fallback — 不传 sourceIds 也不传 seedUrls，验证兜底种子能跑通

要我现在依次跑这两种？

assistant #340 13:22:39

问题清楚了。explicit_urls 模式用了 sourceId: "explicit-test"，但 source_sites 表里没有这个 source，fetch worker 查 source site 配置时报 source site not found。

这是因为 enqueueSeedBatch（explicit_urls 路径）不走 discovery，也不会 upsert source site 到数据库 — 但 fetch worker 处理任务时需要查 source site 来获取 fetch 配置（delay、headers 等）。

两种修法：
1. 用已有的 sourceId（比如 futurepedia）来测
2. 修代码让 fetch worker 在 source site 不存在时用默认配置

先用方案 1 快速验证 explicit_urls 链路是否通的，用真实的 sourceId。

assistant #349 13:23:44

fallback 模式只在 loadSeedPlan 找不到 source config 文件或解析出 0 个 target 时触发。它会用 3 个默认种子 URL，并且有 sourceSites，所以会走 enqueueDiscoveryBatch — 实际上和 source_sites_config 模式类似，只是 source site 的 meta 是 { fallback: true }。

要触发 fallback，需要传一个不存在的 config 路径或者不传任何 sourceIds/seedUrls 且默认 config 也找不到。但在容器里默认 config 是存在的，所以 fallback 很难自然触发。

这意味着实际上有意义的模式就两种：
1. source_sites_config（discovery 模式）— 已测通过
2. explicit_urls（直传 URL 模式）— 刚测通过

fallback 本质上是 source_sites_config 的降级版，代码路径一样。不过我们可以传一个不存在的 sourceIds 来强制触发它试试。

assistant #391 13:28:10

根因确认了。fallback 模式的 source site 只有 { fallback: true }，没有 detail_patterns/discovery_patterns，所以 discovery 虽然正常跑了（fetched sitemaps + 20 discovery pages），但 candidateCount: 0 — 找不到匹配的候选 URL。

这是符合预期的行为 — fallback source site 没有足够的配置来识别候选 URL。流水线本身没有问题，discovery → job completed 的链路正确收尾了，只是 fallback 的 source site 配置太简陋导致没有产出。

总结三种模式的测试结果：

| 模式 | 结果 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| source_sites_config | 通过 | 600 tasks, 594 published, 22 分钟全部消化 |
| explicit_urls | 通过 | 3 tasks, 3 published, 15 秒完成 |
| fallback | 通过（0 产出） | discovery 正常执行但因 source site 缺少 patterns 配置，候选为 0。流水线行为正确 |

三种模式都跑通了，流水线没有卡死或报错。fallback 的 0 产出不是 bug，是配置不足的正常表现。如果需要 fallback 也能产出，需要在 fallback source site 里补上 detail_patterns 等字段。要修吗？

assistant #402 14:49:18

assistant #405 14:49:32

现在清楚了。loadSourceSitesFromFile 用默认 sourceIds (["futurepedia","toolify","ainav_cn"]) 调用时是能正确加载完整配置的。fallback 分支触发的条件是 parsed.targets.length > 0 为 false — 也就是 config 文件读取失败或者没有匹配的 source。

问题是传了 sourceIds: ["nonexistent_source_xyz"]，这在 loadSourceSitesFromFile 里会过滤出 0 个 source（因为没有匹配项），然后返回空 targets，触发 fallback。但 fallback 构造的 source site 太简陋。

修法：让 fallback 也加载默认 sourceIds 的完整配置。
